Dealers will be charged an upgrade fee of $50.00 per customer for SW kit.

|  The list price of Workforce Analytics is $50 per employee. This reflects the value and potential cost savings as well as the time and cost it would take for a customer to build it themselves. # Software - Workforce Integration Manager

Workforce Integration Manager v6 is Kronos' nextgeneration data integration tool, which efficiently interfaces Workforce Central products with other business applications. Like Workforce Connect, Workforce Integration Manager enables users to extract, transfer, share, and perform calculations on data. While Workforce Connect is an entirely Windows client-side utility. Workforce Integration Manager allows users to run and maintain interfaces from within Workforce Central.

# Time and Expense Billable Rates

|   | Software Support |  | Hardware Support |  |   |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
|   | On-Site | Phone Support | On-Site | Phone Support |   |
|  Day and Time (local time) | Minimum Hour |  | Minimum Hours | Minimum Hours | Minimum Hours  |
|  Monday - Friday (8 AM - 5PM) | 4 | 2 |  | 2 | 2  |
|  Monday - Friday (after 5PM) | 6 | 3 |  | 4 | 3  |
|  Weekend \& Holidays | 8 | 6 |  | 6 | 6  |

Please Note: Contract Customers receive a 50\% discount from the minimum amount of hours.

Workforce Analytics - How is the Workforce Analytics Priced? |  |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
The list price of Workforce Analytics is $50 per employee. This reflects the value and potential cost savings as well as the time and cost it would take for a customer to build it themselves. There is a minimum base price of $35,000 that must be reached in each deal for the software license (actual, not list). In other words, if the customer has 1,000 employees and pays $30 per employee after discounts, the software license price would only be $30,000 - the customer must pay the base of $35,000 in license fees. If, however the customer has 2,000 employees the customer would pay $60,000 at $30,000 per employee. Normal discounting rules apply as set out recently. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |

# Software - Workforce Integration Manager

Workforce Integration Manager v6 is Kronos' nextgeneration data integration tool, which efficiently interfaces Workforce Central products with other business applications. Like Workforce Connect, Workforce Integration Manager enables users to extract, transfer, share, and perform calculations on data. While Workforce Connect is an entirely Windows client-side utility. Workforce Integration Manager allows users to run and maintain interfaces from within Workforce Central.

=== TABLE_31 ===
Workforce Analytics - How is the Workforce Analytics Priced? |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
---------------------------------------------------------------------------------------
--- |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
The list price of Workforce Analytics is $50 per employee. This reflects the value and potential cost savings as well as the time and cost it would take for a customer to build it themselves. There is a minimum base price of $35,000 that must be reached in each deal for the software license (actual, not list). In other words, if the customer has 1,000 employees and pays $30 per employee after discounts, the software license price would only be $30,000  the customer must pay the base of $35,000 in license fees. If, however, the customer has 2,000 employees, the customer would pay $60,000 at $30 per employee. Normal discounting rules apply as set out recently. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  | 
Workforce Analytics for Retail follows the same pattern, but costs $60 per employee. Service costs will vary significantly depending on the scope of work, but expect an absolute minimum of $40,000. |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |  |
